local isRunning = false
local animationConnection -- Store the animation event connection
local deathConnection -- Store the death event connection

Tabs.Main:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Dunk",
    Description = "Use Garous Lethal Whirlwind Or Atomics Atmos Cleave",
    Callback = function()

        local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")

        local function sendNotification(title, text)
            StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
                Title = title;
                Text = text;
                Duration = 5; -- Notification duration (in seconds)
            })

        local function unloadScript()
            if animationConnection then
                animationConnection:Disconnect()
                animationConnection = nil
            if deathConnection then
                deathConnection:Disconnect()
                deathConnection = nil
            print("Unloaded Auto Dunk")
            sendNotification("Auto Dunk", "Script has been unloaded.")
            isRunning = false

        if isRunning then
            unloadScript()
        else
            print("Auto Dunk enabled")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")
            local player = Players.LocalPlayer
            local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
            local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

            local validAnimationIds = {
                ["rbxassetid://12296113986"] = 1.1, -- Animation ID with normal wait time
                ["rbxassetid://15145462680"] = 2.0  -- Animation ID with different wait time
            }

            local function teleportUpAndDown()
                local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if rootPart then
                    local originalCFrame = rootPart.CFrame

                    rootPart.CFrame = rootPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 250, 0)
                    
                    wait(0.5)
                    rootPart.CFrame = originalCFrame

            animationConnection = humanoid.AnimationPlayed:Connect(function(animationTrack)
                local animationId = animationTrack.Animation.AnimationId
                if validAnimationIds[animationId] then
                    local waitTime = validAnimationIds[animationId] -- Get the corresponding wait time
                    wait(waitTime) -- Wait for the animation-specific timing
                    teleportUpAndDown() -- Teleport the player up and back down
            end)

            deathConnection = humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                unloadScript()
            end)

            sendNotification("Auto Dunk", "Script is now active.")
            isRunning = true
})

local isRunning = false
local animationConnection -- Store the animation event connection
local deathConnection -- Store the death event connection

Tabs.Main:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Extender",
    Description = "Use Garous Hunters Grasp, Rock Splitting Fist Or Metal Bats Foul Ball",
    Callback = function()

        local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")

        local function sendNotification(title, text)
            StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
                Title = title;
                Text = text;
                Duration = 5; -- Notification duration (in seconds)
            })

        local function unloadScript()
            if animationConnection then
                animationConnection:Disconnect()
                animationConnection = nil
            if deathConnection then
                deathConnection:Disconnect()
                deathConnection = nil
            print("Unloaded Auto Extender")
            sendNotification("Auto Extender", "Script has been unloaded.")
            isRunning = false

        if isRunning then
            unloadScript()
        else
            print("Auto Extender enabled")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")
            local player = Players.LocalPlayer
            local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
            local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

            local validAnimationIds = {
                ["rbxassetid://12309835105"] = 0.5, -- Animation ID with normal wait time
                ["rbxassetid://14057231976"] = 1,  -- Animation ID with different wait time
                ["rbxassetid://14705929107"] = 1.8,  -- Animation ID with different wait time
            }

            local function teleportUpGroundAndForward()
                local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if rootPart then
                    local forwardDirection = rootPart.CFrame.LookVector

                    local originalCFrame = rootPart.CFrame

                    rootPart.CFrame = rootPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 125, 0)

                    wait(0.5)

                    rootPart.CFrame = originalCFrame

                    rootPart.CFrame = rootPart.CFrame + forwardDirection * 125

            animationConnection = humanoid.AnimationPlayed:Connect(function(animationTrack)
                local animationId = animationTrack.Animation.AnimationId
                if validAnimationIds[animationId] then
                    local waitTime = validAnimationIds[animationId] -- Get the corresponding wait time
                    wait(waitTime) -- Wait for the animation-specific timing
                    teleportUpGroundAndForward() -- Teleport the player up, to ground, and forward
            end)

            deathConnection = humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                unloadScript()
            end)

            sendNotification("Auto Extender", "Script is now active.")
            isRunning = true
})

Tabs.Anti:AddButton({
    Title = "Anti Death Counter",
    Description = "Bypasses Death Counter",
    Callback = function()
        local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")

        local function sendNotification(title, text)
            StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
                Title = title;
                Text = text;
                Duration = 5; -- Notification duration (in seconds)
            })

        local function unloadScript()
            if connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            if deathConnection then
                deathConnection:Disconnect()
            print("Unloaded")
            sendNotification("Anti Death Counter", "Script has been unloaded.")
            isRunning = false

            unloadScript()

            local animationID = "11343250001"

            local function isAnimationPlaying(animTrack, id)
                return animTrack and animTrack.Animation.AnimationId == "rbxassetid://" .. id

            local function findClosestPlayer()
                local closestPlayer = nil
                local shortestDistance = math.huge

                for _, otherPlayer in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if otherPlayer ~= player and otherPlayer.Character and otherPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        local distance = (character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - otherPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                        if distance < shortestDistance then
                            shortestDistance = distance
                            closestPlayer = otherPlayer

                return closestPlayer

            local function monitorAnimations()
                connection = humanoid.AnimationPlayed:Connect(function(animTrack)
                    if isAnimationPlaying(animTrack, animationID) then
                        local originalPosition = character.HumanoidRootPart.Position
                        local originalOrientation = character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame

                        local targetPosition = Vector3.new(1187.54102, -499.052856, 23674.498)
                        local targetOrientation = CFrame.new(
                            1187.54102, -499.052856, 23674.498,  -- Position
                            0.747619033, -6.86524757e-08, -0.664127827,  -- Orientation Matrix
                            2.13483915e-08, 1, -7.93401611e-08,
                            0.664127827, 4.51381545e-08, 0.747619033
                        )

                        local function spawnPart()
                            local part = Instance.new("Part")
                            part.Size = Vector3.new(500, 1, 500)
                            part.Anchored = true
                            part.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPosition)
                            part.Parent = workspace
                            return part

                        local function teleportToTarget()
                            if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                local standPosition = targetPosition + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0) -- 2 units above the part
                                local standOrientation = CFrame.new(
                                    standPosition,
                                    standPosition + targetOrientation.LookVector
                                )
                                character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = standOrientation

                        local function chatMessage(str)
                            str = tostring(str)
                            local TextChatService = game:GetService("TextChatService")
                            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

                            if TextChatService.ChatVersion == Enum.ChatVersion.TextChatService then
                                TextChatService.TextChannels.RBXGeneral:SendAsync(str)
                            else
                                ReplicatedStorage.DefaultChatSystemChatEvents.SayMessageRequest:FireServer(str, "All")

                        local messages = {

                        local unusedMessages = {}

                        local function shuffle(tbl)
                            local len = #tbl
                            for i = len, 2, -1 do
                                local j = math.random(1, i)
                                tbl[i], tbl[j] = tbl[j], tbl[i]

                        local function resetMessages()
                            unusedMessages = {unpack(messages)}
                            shuffle(unusedMessages)

                        resetMessages()

                        local function sendUniqueMessage()
                            if #unusedMessages == 0 then
                                resetMessages()  -- Refill and shuffle when all messages have been used

                            local message = table.remove(unusedMessages, 1)

                            if string.find(message, "Death Counterer") then

                                    local displayName = closestPlayer.DisplayName or closestPlayer.Name

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local function fixCamera()
    local camera = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera
    local savedCFrame = camera.CFrame -- Save the camera's CFrame before destroying it
    
    camera:Destroy() -- Destroy the current camera
    
    local char = player.Character
    if char then
        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildWhichIsA('Humanoid')
        if humanoid then
            local newCamera = Instance.new("Camera")
            newCamera.Parent = game.Workspace
            game.Workspace.CurrentCamera = newCamera
            newCamera.CameraSubject = humanoid
            newCamera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Custom
            newCamera.CFrame = savedCFrame -- Restore the saved CFrame
            
            player.CameraMinZoomDistance = 0.5
            player.CameraMaxZoomDistance = 400
            player.CameraMode = Enum.CameraMode.Classic
            
            if char:FindFirstChild("Head") then
                char.Head.Anchored = false

fixCamera()

                        local standPart = spawnPart()
                        teleportToTarget()

                        wait(2)
                        teleportBack()
                end)

            deathConnection = humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                unloadScript()
            end)

            monitorAnimations()

            sendNotification("Anti Death Counter", "Script is now active.")
            isRunning = true
})

local Toggle = Tabs.Main:AddToggle("InfJumpToggle", {
    Title = "Inf Jump",
    Description = "Self Explantory",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(A)
        _G.infinjump = not _G.infinjump

        if _G.infinJumpStarted == nil then
            _G.infinJumpStarted = true
            
            local plr = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
            local m = plr:GetMouse()
            m.KeyDown:Connect(function(k)
                if _G.infinjump then
                    if k:byte() == 32 then
                        local humanoid = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid')
                        humanoid:ChangeState('Jumping')
                        wait()
                        humanoid:ChangeState('Seated')
            end)
})

Toggle:SetValue(false)  -- Set the initial state to false

local resurrectionToggled = false

local Toggle = Tabs.Main:AddToggle("ResurrectionToggle", {
    Title = "Resurrection",
    Description = "Spawns You Where You Last Died",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        resurrectionToggled = Value
    end,
})

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local lp = Players.LocalPlayer

local oldCFrame

local function onCharacterRemoving(char)
    if resurrectionToggled then
        local root = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if root then
            oldCFrame = root.CFrame

local function onCharacterAdded(char)
    if resurrectionToggled and oldCFrame then
        local newRoot = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 5) -- Timeout for safety
        if newRoot then
            newRoot.CFrame = oldCFrame

local function chatMessage(str)
    str = tostring(str)
    local TextChatService = game:GetService("TextChatService")
    local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

    if TextChatService.ChatVersion == Enum.ChatVersion.TextChatService then
        TextChatService.TextChannels.RBXGeneral:SendAsync(str)
    else
        ReplicatedStorage.DefaultChatSystemChatEvents.SayMessageRequest:FireServer(str, "All")

local unusedMessages = {}

local function shuffle(tbl)
    local len = #tbl
    for i = len, 2, -1 do
        local j = math.random(1, i)
        tbl[i], tbl[j] = tbl[j], tbl[i]

local function resetMessages()
    unusedMessages = {unpack(messages)}
    shuffle(unusedMessages)

resetMessages()

local chanceToSendMessage = 1

local function sendUniqueMessage()
    if math.random() <= chanceToSendMessage then
        if #unusedMessages == 0 then
            resetMessages()  -- Refill and shuffle when all messages have been used
        
        local message = table.remove(unusedMessages, 1)
        chatMessage(message)

sendUniqueMessage()

local animations = {
    "15957361339", -- Replace with your first Animation ID
    "15957376722", -- Replace with your second Animation ID
    "17106169665", -- Replace with your third Animation ID
    "18435303746",
}

local playedAnimations = {}

local function getRandomUnplayedAnimationId()
    if #playedAnimations == #animations then
        playedAnimations = {} -- Reset the played animations if all have been played

    local availableAnimations = {}

    for _, animationId in ipairs(animations) do
        if not table.find(playedAnimations, animationId) then
            table.insert(availableAnimations, animationId)

    local randomAnimationId = availableAnimations[math.random(1, #availableAnimations)]

    table.insert(playedAnimations, randomAnimationId)

    return randomAnimationId

local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()

local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

local function playRandomAnimation()
    local randomAnimationId = getRandomUnplayedAnimationId()

    local animation = Instance.new("Animation")
    animation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. randomAnimationId

    local animationTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(animation)
    animationTrack:Play()

playRandomAnimation()

local Keybind = Tabs.Bind:AddKeybind("Keybind", {
    Title = "Anime Tp Keybind",
    Mode = "Hold",
    Default = "LeftAlt",
    ChangedCallback = function(New)
        keybindKey = New  -- Update the keybindKey to the new key
        print("Keybind changed:", New)
})

Toggle:OnChanged(function(ToggleValue)
    teleportEnabled = ToggleValue

    if teleportEnabled then
        local targetAnimationIds = { "13071982935", "16746824621", "13073745835" } -- Add multiple target animation IDs here
        local restrictedAnimationId = "15957361339" -- The ID of the animation you don't want to play
        local animationDuration = 3 -- Time in seconds
        local animationSpeed = 2 -- Speed of the animation

        local function detectTargetAnimation(character)
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if humanoid then
                for _, track in ipairs(humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                    for _, targetId in ipairs(targetAnimationIds) do
                        if track.Animation.AnimationId == "rbxassetid://" .. targetId then
                            return true -- Target animation detected
            return false

        local function playEffects(character)
            local ss = game:GetService("SoundService")
            local Sound = Instance.new("Sound", ss)
            Sound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://5066021887"
            Sound.Volume = 1
            Sound.Pitch = math.random(80, 120) / 100 -- Adjusted to vary pitch
            Sound:Play()

            local humanoidRootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

            local function findDescendant(parent, name)
                local child = parent:FindFirstChild(name)
                if not child then
                    for _, descendant in ipairs(parent:GetChildren()) do
                        child = findDescendant(descendant, name)
                        if child then
                            break
                return child

            local function duplicateEmitter(originalEmitter)
                local duplicate = originalEmitter:Clone()
                duplicate.Parent = originalEmitter.Parent
                duplicate.Rate = 150  -- Set the rate of the duplicated emitter to 150 initially
                return duplicate

            local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local resourcesFolder = replicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Resources", 2) -- Wait for 2 seconds if not immediately found
            if resourcesFolder then
                local kjEffectsFolder = resourcesFolder:FindFirstChild("KJEffects")
                if kjEffectsFolder then
                    local tpThingEmitter = findDescendant(kjEffectsFolder, "tpthing")
                    if tpThingEmitter and tpThingEmitter:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
                        local duplicatedEmitter = duplicateEmitter(tpThingEmitter)

                        duplicatedEmitter.Parent = humanoidRootPart

                        local invisibilityDuration = .4 -- Time the player stays invisible (in seconds)
                        local invisibleTransparency = 1 -- Transparency when invisible (0 is fully visible, 1 is fully invisible)
                        local visibleTransparency = 0 -- Transparency when visible (0 is fully visible)

                        local excludedParts = {
                            "HumanoidRootPart",
                            "Hitbox_RightArm",
                            "Hitbox_RightLeg",
                            "Hitbox_LeftLeg",
                            "Hitbox_LeftArm",
                            "camera",
                            "camerarootpart",
                            "letterboxtop",
                            "letterboxbot",
                            "Cylinder.002",
                            "Cylinder.005",
                            "Cylinder.006",
                            "Main",
                            "Circle.002",
                            "Circle.001",
                            "Circle",
                            "Cylinder",
                            "Cylinder.003",
                            "Cylinder.010",
                            "WeaponHold",
                        }

                        local function isExcluded(part)
                            for _, name in ipairs(excludedParts) do
                                if part.Name == name then
                                    return true
                            return false

                        local function turnInvisible()
                            for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                                if part:IsA("BasePart") and not isExcluded(part) then
                                    part.Transparency = invisibleTransparency
                                elseif (part:IsA("Decal") or part:IsA("Texture")) and not isExcluded(part.Parent) then
                                    part.Transparency = 1 -- Hide textures/decals fully

                        local function turnVisible()
                            for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                                if part:IsA("BasePart") and not isExcluded(part) then
                                    part.Transparency = visibleTransparency
                                elseif (part:IsA("Decal") or part:IsA("Texture")) and not isExcluded(part.Parent) then
                                    part.Transparency = 0 -- Show textures/decals again

                        turnInvisible()
                        wait(invisibilityDuration)
                        turnVisible()

                        duplicatedEmitter.Rate = 0
                    else
                        warn("Could not find tpthing ParticleEmitter or it is not a ParticleEmitter.")
                else
                    warn("Could not find KJEffects folder inside Resources.")
            else
                warn("Could not find Resources folder inside ReplicatedStorage.")

        local function playAnimation(character, speed, duration)
            if detectTargetAnimation(character) then
                warn("Target animation detected, restricting animation playback.")
                playEffects(character)
                return -- Exit function if target animation is detected

            local animation = Instance.new("Animation")
            animation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. restrictedAnimationId

            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if humanoid then
                local animationTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(animation)
                animationTrack:Play()

                playEffects(character)

                animationTrack:AdjustSpeed(speed or 2)

                wait(duration or animationDuration)
                animationTrack:Stop()

        local function teleportToMouse()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local mouse = player:GetMouse()
            if mouse then
                local mouseHit = mouse.Hit
                if mouseHit then
                    player.Character:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(mouseHit.p))

                    local character = player.Character
                    if character then
                        playAnimation(character, animationSpeed, animationDuration)

        inputConnection = game:GetService("UserInputService").InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if teleportEnabled and input.KeyCode == keybindKey then
                teleportToMouse()
        end)
    else
        if inputConnection then
            inputConnection:Disconnect()
            inputConnection = nil
end)

local TextChatService = game:GetService("TextChatService")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local SacredSummoningNameInput = Tabs.Settings:AddInput("SacredSummoningNameInput", {
    Title = "Sacred Summoning Name",
    Default = "Default Name",
    Placeholder = "Enter the name for Sacred Summoning",
    Numeric = false, -- Allows both text and numbers
    Finished = true, -- Calls the callback only when you press Enter
    Callback = function(Value)
        print("Sacred Summoning Name changed:", Value)
})

Tabs.tool:AddButton({
    Title = "WITH THIS SACRED TREASURE I SUMMON",
    Description = "Gives the Sacred Summoning tool",
    Callback = function()
        local animationId = "17862993552"

        local currentAnimationTrack

        local function chatMessage(str)
            str = tostring(str)
            if TextChatService.ChatVersion == Enum.ChatVersion.TextChatService then
                TextChatService.TextChannels.RBXGeneral:SendAsync(str)
            else
                ReplicatedStorage.DefaultChatSystemChatEvents.SayMessageRequest:FireServer(str, "All")

        local function stopAllAnimations(humanoid)
            for _, track in ipairs(humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                if track ~= currentAnimationTrack then
                    track:Stop() -- Stop all other animations

        local function playAnimation(character)
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if not humanoid then return end

            if currentAnimationTrack then
                currentAnimationTrack:Stop()

            local animation = Instance.new("Animation")
            animation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. animationId

            currentAnimationTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(animation)

            currentAnimationTrack:Play()

        local function createCompoundVTool()
            local tool = Instance.new("Tool")
            tool.Name = "Sacred Summoning"
            tool.RequiresHandle = false
            tool.CanBeDropped = false
            
            tool.Equipped:Connect(function()
                local character = Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                if not character then return end

                local summoningName = (SacredSummoningNameInput.Value or "UNKNOWN NAME"):upper() .. "!"

                playAnimation(character)

                chatMessage("WITH THIS SACRED TREASURE I SUMMON " .. summoningName)
            end)

            tool.Unequipped:Connect(function()
                local character = Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                if not character then return end

                if currentAnimationTrack then
                    currentAnimationTrack:Stop()
                    currentAnimationTrack = nil
                
                local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                if humanoid then
                    humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16 -- Reset to default walk speed
            end)

            tool.Parent = Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack

        createCompoundVTool() -- Create and give the Sacred Summoning tool
    end,
})

Tabs.tool:AddButton({
    Title = "Sandevistan",
    Description = "Gives the Sandevistan tool--From Cyberpunk(wip)",
    Callback = function() 
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local Lighting = game:GetService("Lighting") -- Include Lighting service
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService") -- For handling key input

local afterimageInterval = 0.05 -- More frequent afterimages for higher density
local afterimageLifetime = 1 -- Longer lifetime to keep afterimages on-screen longer
local transparencyStart = 0.3 -- Less transparent initially for clearer afterimages
local transparencyEnd = 1 -- Fully transparent at the end
local isAfterimageActive = false
local movementThreshold = 0.1 -- Minimum movement to create afterimages
local desiredSpeed = 70 -- Set desired speed
local newAnimationId = "18897115785" -- Animation ID to play when moving
local targetAnimationId = "7815618175" -- Animation ID to stop when moving
local newAnimationTrack -- Variable to hold the new animation track
local originalWalkSpeed -- Variable to store the original walk speed
local speedChangeConnection -- Connection for walk speed change prevention
local animationPlayedConnection -- Connection for the animation played event
local cameraEffect -- Variable to hold the camera effect

local bodyParts = {"Head", "HumanoidRootPart", "Left Arm", "Right Arm", "Left Leg", "Right Leg", "Torso"}

local function hsvToRgb(h, s, v)
    local r, g, b
    local i = math.floor(h * 6)
    local f = h * 6 - i
    local p = v * (1 - s)
    local q = v * (1 - f * s)
    local t = v * (1 - (1 - f) * s)

    i = i % 6
    if i == 0 then r, g, b = v, t, p
    elseif i == 1 then r, g, b = q, v, p
    elseif i == 2 then r, g, b = p, v, t
    elseif i == 3 then r, g, b = p, q, v
    elseif i == 4 then r, g, b = t, p, v
    elseif i == 5 then r, g, b = v, p, q
    return Color3.new(r, g, b)

local function createAfterimageForPart(part, color)
    if not part or not part:IsA("BasePart") then return end

    local afterimagePart = Instance.new("Part")
    afterimagePart.Size = part.Size
    afterimagePart.CFrame = part.CFrame
    afterimagePart.Transparency = transparencyStart
    afterimagePart.Anchored = true
    afterimagePart.CanCollide = false
    afterimagePart.Material = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic -- Set to SmoothPlastic
    afterimagePart.Color = color -- Apply the rainbow color

    if part:FindFirstChildOfClass("SpecialMesh") then
        local mesh = part:FindFirstChildOfClass("SpecialMesh"):Clone()
        mesh.Parent = afterimagePart

    afterimagePart.Parent = workspace

    local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(afterimageLifetime, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
    local tween = TweenService:Create(afterimagePart, tweenInfo, {Transparency = transparencyEnd})
    tween:Play()

    tween.Completed:Connect(function()
        afterimagePart:Destroy()
    end)

local function cloneClothing(character, afterimageClone)
    local shirt = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Shirt")
    if shirt then
        local shirtClone = shirt:Clone()
        shirtClone.Parent = afterimageClone

    local pants = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Pants")
    if pants then
        local pantsClone = pants:Clone()
        pantsClone.Parent = afterimageClone

local function createAfterimageModel(character, color)
    local afterimageClone = Instance.new("Model")
    afterimageClone.Name = "AfterimageClone"
    
    for _, partName in ipairs(bodyParts) do
        local part = character:FindFirstChild(partName)
        if part then
            createAfterimageForPart(part, color)

    cloneClothing(character, afterimageClone)

    afterimageClone.Parent = workspace

local function isCharacterMoving(character)
    local humanoidRootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if humanoidRootPart then
        local velocity = humanoidRootPart.Velocity
        return velocity.Magnitude > movementThreshold
    return false

local function onAnimationPlayed(animationTrack)
    if animationTrack and animationTrack.Animation and animationTrack.Animation.AnimationId == "rbxassetid://" .. targetAnimationId then
        animationTrack:Stop() -- Stop the target animation

local function startAfterimageEffect(character)
    if isAfterimageActive then return end
    isAfterimageActive = true
    local lastSpawnTime = 0

    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if humanoid then
        animationPlayedConnection = humanoid.AnimationPlayed:Connect(onAnimationPlayed)

        RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
            if isAfterimageActive then
                if isCharacterMoving(character) then
                    for _, track in ipairs(humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                        if track.Animation.AnimationId == "rbxassetid://" .. targetAnimationId then
                            track:Stop()
                    
                    if not newAnimationTrack or not newAnimationTrack.IsPlaying then
                        local newAnimation = Instance.new("Animation")
                        newAnimation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. newAnimationId
                        newAnimationTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(newAnimation)
                        newAnimationTrack:Play()
                else
                    if newAnimationTrack and newAnimationTrack.IsPlaying then
                        newAnimationTrack:Stop()
        end)

        RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
            if isAfterimageActive and isCharacterMoving(character) then
                if tick() - lastSpawnTime >= afterimageInterval then
                    local time = tick() % 5 -- A smooth cycle that repeats every 5 seconds
                    local hue = (time / 5) % 1 -- Convert time to a hue value (0 to 1)
                    local color = hsvToRgb(hue, 1, 1) -- Full saturation and brightness
                    
                    createAfterimageModel(character, color)
                    lastSpawnTime = tick() -- Update last spawn time
        end)

local function stopAfterimageEffect()
    isAfterimageActive = false
    if newAnimationTrack then
        newAnimationTrack:Stop()
        newAnimationTrack = nil

    if animationPlayedConnection then
        animationPlayedConnection:Disconnect()
        animationPlayedConnection = nil

local function setPlayerSpeed(speed)
    local character = Players.LocalPlayer.Character
    if character then
        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        if humanoid then
            originalWalkSpeed = humanoid.WalkSpeed -- Store the original walk speed
            humanoid.WalkSpeed = speed

            if speedChangeConnection then
                speedChangeConnection:Disconnect() -- Disconnect previous connection if it exists
            
            speedChangeConnection = humanoid:GetPropertyChangedSignal("WalkSpeed"):Connect(function()
                if humanoid.WalkSpeed ~= speed then
                    humanoid.WalkSpeed = speed
            end)

local function applyCameraEffect()
    local colorCorrection = Instance.new("ColorCorrectionEffect")
    colorCorrection.TintColor = Color3.new(0.1, 0.3, 0.1) -- Slightly dark green tint
    colorCorrection.Brightness = 0.1 -- Adjust brightness
    colorCorrection.Contrast = 0.2 -- Adjust contrast
    colorCorrection.Saturation = 0 -- Optional: adjust saturation
    colorCorrection.Parent = Lighting -- Apply to Lighting
    return colorCorrection

local function removeCameraEffect()
    local existingEffect = Lighting:FindFirstChildOfClass("ColorCorrectionEffect")
    if existingEffect then
        existingEffect:Destroy()

local function chatMessage(str)
    local TextChatService = game:GetService("TextChatService")
    local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

    if TextChatService.ChatVersion == Enum.ChatVersion.TextChatService then
        TextChatService.TextChannels.RBXGeneral:SendAsync(str)
    else
        ReplicatedStorage.DefaultChatSystemChatEvents.SayMessageRequest:FireServer(str, "All")

local function createAfterImagesTool()
    local tool = Instance.new("Tool")
    tool.Name = "Sandevistan"
    tool.RequiresHandle = false
    tool.CanBeDropped = false

    tool.Equipped:Connect(function()
        setPlayerSpeed(desiredSpeed)

        local player = Players.LocalPlayer
        local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
        if not character then return end

        startAfterimageEffect(character)

        cameraEffect = applyCameraEffect()

        chatMessage("Time to chrome the hell up! || é‹¼ã®ã‚ˆã†ã«å¼·ããªã‚‹æ™‚ã ï¼")

        tool.Unequipped:Connect(function()
            stopAfterimageEffect()
            if character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") then
                local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16 -- Reset speed to normal
                if speedChangeConnection then
                    speedChangeConnection:Disconnect() -- Disconnect speed change prevention
                    speedChangeConnection = nil
            
            if cameraEffect then
                removeCameraEffect() -- Ensure the effect is removed
        end)
    end)

    UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
        if gameProcessed then return end -- Ignore if the input is processed by the game
        
        if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.R then
            local player = Players.LocalPlayer
            local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
            if not character then return end

            if isAfterimageActive then
                stopAfterimageEffect()
                if character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") then
                    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                    humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16 -- Reset speed to normal
                    if speedChangeConnection then
                        speedChangeConnection:Disconnect() -- Disconnect speed change prevention
                        speedChangeConnection = nil
                removeCameraEffect() -- Remove camera effect
            else
                startAfterimageEffect(character)
                setPlayerSpeed(desiredSpeed)

                cameraEffect = applyCameraEffect()
        		chatMessage("Time to chrome the hell up! || é‹¼ã®ã‚ˆã†ã«å¼·ããªã‚‹æ™‚ã ï¼")
    end)

    tool.Parent = Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack")

createAfterImagesTool()

    end,
})

Tabs.tool:AddButton({
    Title = "Flashstep",
    Description = "Gives the flashstep tool",
    Callback = function() 
local function initiateRush()
    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
    local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
    local rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if not humanoid then return end

    local animation = Instance.new("Animation")
    animation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://17838006839"  -- Your provided animation ID
    local animationTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(animation)

    local rushSpeed = 100
    local maxForce = Vector3.new(100000, 0, 100000)  -- Adjust max force as needed
    local rushDirection = Vector3.new(rootPart.CFrame.LookVector.X, 0, rootPart.CFrame.LookVector.Z).unit  -- Ignore Y direction

    local bodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
    bodyVelocity.Velocity = rushDirection * rushSpeed
    bodyVelocity.MaxForce = maxForce
    bodyVelocity.P = 10000  -- Adjust P value for smoother movement
    bodyVelocity.Parent = rootPart

    local function updateRushDirection()
        rushDirection = Vector3.new(rootPart.CFrame.LookVector.X, 0, rootPart.CFrame.LookVector.Z).unit
        bodyVelocity.Velocity = rushDirection * rushSpeed

    local connection = game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(updateRushDirection)

    local isAnimating = true
    local rushDuration = 4.15  -- Total duration of the rush effect
    local timePassed = 0  -- Time tracker
    local lastCycleFinished = false  -- Tracks if the last animation cycle is finishing
    coroutine.wrap(function()
        while isAnimating and timePassed < rushDuration do
            if rushDuration - timePassed <= 1 then
                animationTrack:Play()  -- Play the animation
                lastCycleFinished = true  -- Mark the last cycle as running
                break  -- Exit the loop to allow animation to finish naturally
            else
                animationTrack:Play()
                wait(0.6)  -- Wait for 0.5 seconds
                animationTrack:Stop()  -- Stop the animation
            wait(0.01)  -- Small wait before the next cycle
            timePassed = timePassed + 1.01  -- Track time to know when to let the animation finish
    end)()

    local humanoidRootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

    local function findDescendant(parent, name)
        local child = parent:FindFirstChild(name)
        if not child then
            for _, descendant in ipairs(parent:GetChildren()) do
                child = findDescendant(descendant, name)
                if child then
                    break
        return child

    local function duplicateEmitter(originalEmitter)
        local duplicate = originalEmitter:Clone()
        duplicate.Parent = originalEmitter.Parent
        duplicate.Rate = 150  -- Set the rate of the duplicated emitter to 150 initially
        return duplicate

    local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
    local resourcesFolder = replicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Resources", 2) -- Wait for 2 seconds if not immediately found
    if resourcesFolder then
        local kjEffectsFolder = resourcesFolder:FindFirstChild("KJEffects")
        if kjEffectsFolder then
            local tpThingEmitter = findDescendant(kjEffectsFolder, "tpthing")
            if tpThingEmitter and tpThingEmitter:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
                local duplicatedEmitter = duplicateEmitter(tpThingEmitter)

                duplicatedEmitter.Parent = humanoidRootPart

                local invisibleTransparency = 1 -- Transparency when invisible (1 is fully invisible)
                local visibleTransparency = 0 -- Transparency when visible (0 is fully visible)

                local excludedParts = {
                    "HumanoidRootPart",
                    "Hitbox_RightArm",
                    "Hitbox_RightLeg",
                    "Hitbox_LeftLeg",
                    "Hitbox_LeftArm",
                    "camera",
                    "camerarootpart",
                    "letterboxtop",
                    "letterboxbot",
                    "Cylinder.002",
                    "Cylinder.005",
                    "Cylinder.006",
                    "Main",
                    "Circle.002",
                    "Circle.001",
                    "Circle",
                    "Cylinder",
                    "Cylinder.003",
                    "Cylinder.010",
                    "WeaponHold",
                }

                local function isExcluded(part)
                    for _, name in ipairs(excludedParts) do
                        if part.Name == name then
                            return true
                    return false

                local function turnInvisible()
                    for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                        if part:IsA("BasePart") and not isExcluded(part) then
                            part.Transparency = invisibleTransparency
                        elseif (part:IsA("Decal") or part:IsA("Texture")) and not isExcluded(part.Parent) then
                            part.Transparency = 1 -- Hide textures/decals fully

                local function turnVisible()
                    for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                        if part:IsA("BasePart") and not isExcluded(part) then
                            part.Transparency = visibleTransparency
                        elseif (part:IsA("Decal") or part:IsA("Texture")) and not isExcluded(part.Parent) then
                            part.Transparency = 0 -- Show textures/decals again

                local isRushing = true
                coroutine.wrap(function()
                    while isRushing do
                        duplicatedEmitter.Rate = 150
                        turnInvisible()

                        wait(0.4) -- Stay invisible and emit particles for 0.4 seconds

                        duplicatedEmitter.Rate = 0
                        turnVisible()

                        wait(0.01) -- Remain visible for 0.6 seconds (total cycle time = 1 second)
                end)()

                local function stopRushEffect()
                    bodyVelocity:Destroy()
                    connection:Disconnect()
                    isRushing = false  -- Stop the particle effect
                    duplicatedEmitter:Destroy()  -- Clean up the emitter

                    if lastCycleFinished then
                        animationTrack.Stopped:Wait()  -- Wait for the last animation to fully finish

                    isAnimating = false  -- Stop the animation cycling

                wait(4.15)
                stopRushEffect()
            else
                warn("Could not find tpthing ParticleEmitter or it is not a ParticleEmitter.")
        else
            warn("Could not find KJEffects folder inside Resources.")
    else
        warn("Could not find Resources folder inside ReplicatedStorage.")

local function createCompoundVTool()
    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
    local tool = Instance.new("Tool")
    tool.Name = "Flash Step"
    tool.RequiresHandle = false
    tool.CanBeDropped = false
    tool.Parent = player.Backpack
    
    local canUse = true  -- Cooldown flag

    tool.Equipped:Connect(function()
        if not canUse then
            print("You must wait for the cooldown!")
            return

        local character = player.Character
        if not character then return end

        initiateRush()
        
        canUse = false
        wait(1)  -- 1-second cooldown
        canUse = true
    end)

    tool.Unequipped:Connect(function()
        local character = player.Character
        if not character then return end

    end)

createCompoundVTool()

    end,
})

Tabs.tool:AddButton({
    Title = "Evade",
    Description = "Gives the Evade tool and enables running animation",
    Callback = function() 
local animationIdRight = "13498257044" -- Animation ID for the right rush
local animationIdLeft = "13498256004" -- Animation ID for the left rush

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

local afterimageInterval = 0.04 -- Increased interval to reduce density (less frequent afterimages)
local afterimageLifetime = 0.25 -- Shorter lifetime to clear out afterimages faster
local transparencyStart = 0.7 -- More transparent from the start
local transparencyEnd = 1 -- Fully transparent at the end
local isAfterimageActive = false -- Track if the effect is active
local movementThreshold = 0.1 -- Minimum movement required to spawn afterimages
local animationSpeed = 2.5 -- Animation speed (can be adjusted as needed)
local cooldownTime = 1 -- Cooldown time in seconds
local lastUsedTime = 0 -- Track last use time

local bodyParts = {"Head", "HumanoidRootPart", "Left Arm", "Right Arm", "Left Leg", "Right Leg", "Torso"}

local function createAfterimageForPart(part)
    local afterimagePart = Instance.new("Part")
    afterimagePart.Size = part.Size
    afterimagePart.CFrame = part.CFrame
    afterimagePart.Transparency = transparencyStart
    afterimagePart.Anchored = true
    afterimagePart.CanCollide = false
    afterimagePart.Material = Enum.Material.Neon -- Make it glow
    afterimagePart.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Institutional white") -- Set color to white
    afterimagePart.Parent = workspace

    local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(afterimageLifetime, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
    local tween = TweenService:Create(afterimagePart, tweenInfo, {Transparency = transparencyEnd})
    tween:Play()

    tween.Completed:Connect(function()
        afterimagePart:Destroy()
    end)

local function createAfterimages(character)
    for _, partName in ipairs(bodyParts) do
        local part = character:FindFirstChild(partName)
        if part then
            createAfterimageForPart(part)

local function isCharacterMoving(character)
    local humanoidRootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if humanoidRootPart then
        local velocity = humanoidRootPart.Velocity
        return velocity.Magnitude > movementThreshold
    return false

local function startAfterimageEffect(character)
    isAfterimageActive = true
    local lastSpawnTime = 0 -- Initialize last spawn time

    RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if isAfterimageActive and isCharacterMoving(character) then
            if tick() - lastSpawnTime >= afterimageInterval then
                createAfterimages(character)
                lastSpawnTime = tick() -- Update last spawn time
    end)

local function stopAfterimageEffect()
    isAfterimageActive = false

local function initiateRush()
    local player = Players.LocalPlayer
    local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
    local rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if not humanoid then return end

    local rushSound = Instance.new("Sound")
    rushSound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://2162239324"
    rushSound.Volume = 1 -- Adjust the volume if needed
    rushSound.PlayOnRemove = false
    rushSound.Parent = rootPart
    rushSound:Play()

    local rushSpeed = 100
    local maxForce = Vector3.new(100000, 0, 100000)  -- Adjust max force as needed

    local randomDirection = math.random(0, 1) -- 0 for left, 1 for right
    local rushDirection

    local animation
    if randomDirection == 0 then
        rushDirection = -rootPart.CFrame.RightVector.unit -- Left direction
        animation = Instance.new("Animation")
        animation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. animationIdLeft
    else
        rushDirection = rootPart.CFrame.RightVector.unit -- Right direction
        animation = Instance.new("Animation")
        animation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. animationIdRight

    local animationTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(animation)
    animationTrack.Looped = false -- Ensure the animation does not loop
    animationTrack:Play()
    
    animationTrack:AdjustSpeed(animationSpeed)

    local bodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
    bodyVelocity.Velocity = rushDirection * rushSpeed
    bodyVelocity.MaxForce = maxForce
    bodyVelocity.P = 10000  -- Adjust P value for smoother movement
    bodyVelocity.Parent = rootPart

    local function updateRushDirection()
        if randomDirection == 0 then
            rushDirection = -rootPart.CFrame.RightVector.unit -- Keep left direction
        else
            rushDirection = rootPart.CFrame.RightVector.unit -- Keep right direction
        bodyVelocity.Velocity = rushDirection * rushSpeed

    local connection = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(updateRushDirection)

    local function stopRushEffect()
        bodyVelocity:Destroy() -- Remove BodyVelocity
        connection:Disconnect() -- Disconnect update connection
        rushSound:Destroy() -- Stop and clean up the sound

    wait(0.1) -- Adjust this wait time based on the rush animation length
    stopRushEffect()

local function createAfterImagesTool()
    local tool = Instance.new("Tool")
    tool.Name = "Evade"
    tool.RequiresHandle = false
    tool.CanBeDropped = false

    tool.Equipped:Connect(function()
        local currentTime = tick()
        if currentTime - lastUsedTime < cooldownTime then
            return -- Exit if within cooldown

        lastUsedTime = currentTime -- Update last used time

        local player = Players.LocalPlayer
        local character = player.Character
        if not character then return end
        
	local ss = game:GetService("SoundService")
local Sound = Instance.new("Sound", ss)
Sound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://2162239324"
Sound.Volume = 10
Sound:Play()

        startAfterimageEffect(character)
        
        initiateRush()

        wait(5) -- Adjust this time as needed
        tool:Unequip()
    end)

    tool.Unequipped:Connect(function()
        local player = Players.LocalPlayer
        local character = player.Character
        if not character then return end
        
        stopAfterimageEffect()
    end)

    tool.Parent = Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack")

createAfterImagesTool()

    end,
})

Tabs.tool:AddButton({
    Title = "Fake Omni",
    Description = "Gives the Fake Omni tool",
    Callback = function()
        local Players = game:GetService("Players")
        local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

        local animationId = "13927612951"

        local currentAnimationTrack

        local function stopAllAnimations(humanoid)
            for _, track in ipairs(humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                if track ~= currentAnimationTrack then
                    track:Stop() -- Stop all other animations

        local function playAnimation(character)
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if not humanoid then return end

            if currentAnimationTrack then
                currentAnimationTrack:Stop()

            local animation = Instance.new("Animation")
            animation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. animationId

            currentAnimationTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(animation)

            currentAnimationTrack:Play()

        local function createCompoundVTool()
            local tool = Instance.new("Tool")
            tool.Name = "Fake Omni"
            tool.RequiresHandle = false
            tool.CanBeDropped = false
            
            tool.Equipped:Connect(function()
                local character = Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                if not character then return end

                playAnimation(character)
            end)

            tool.Unequipped:Connect(function()
                local character = Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                if not character then return end

                if currentAnimationTrack then
                    currentAnimationTrack:Stop()
                    currentAnimationTrack = nil
                
                local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                if humanoid then
                    humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16 -- Reset to default walk speed
            end)

            tool.Parent = Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack

        createCompoundVTool() -- Create and give the Compound V tool
    end,
})

Tabs.CustomMovesets:AddButton({
    Title = "Pressurizer",
    Description = "Use Saitama--First Moveset I made--MycroMan",
   Callback = function()
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local camera = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera
local playerGui = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")

local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local humanoidRootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

local cutsceneDuration = 1
local fadeDuration = 1

local screenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui", playerGui)
local frame = Instance.new("Frame", screenGui)
frame.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
frame.Size = UDim2.new(900, 0, 900, 0) -- Set the size to be 900 times bigger
frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1

local textLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", screenGui)
textLabel.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
textLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
textLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0.2, 0, 0.1, 0)
textLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
textLabel.Text = "åŠ åœ§å™¨"
textLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 0, 0) -- Set text color to red
textLabel.TextScaled = true
textLabel.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
textLabel.TextTransparency = 1

local fadeInInfo = TweenInfo.new(
    fadeDuration, -- Time
    Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, -- EasingStyle
    Enum.EasingDirection.InOut -- EasingDirection
)

local fadeOutInfo = TweenInfo.new(
    fadeDuration, -- Time
    Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, -- EasingStyle
    Enum.EasingDirection.InOut -- EasingDirection
)

local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(
    cutsceneDuration, -- Time
    Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, -- EasingStyle
    Enum.EasingDirection.InOut -- EasingDirection
)

local initialCFrame = humanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -5, 0)
local finalCFrame = humanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 2, 2) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(180), 0)

local cameraTween = TweenService:Create(camera, tweenInfo, {CFrame = finalCFrame})

local fadeInTween = TweenService:Create(frame, fadeInInfo, {BackgroundTransparency = 0})
local fadeOutTween = TweenService:Create(frame, fadeOutInfo, {BackgroundTransparency = 1})

local textFadeInTween = TweenService:Create(textLabel, fadeInInfo, {TextTransparency = 0})
local textFadeOutTween = TweenService:Create(textLabel, fadeOutInfo, {TextTransparency = 1})

local function playCutscene()
    camera.CFrame = initialCFrame
    
    fadeInTween:Play()
    textFadeInTween:Play()
    fadeInTween.Completed:Wait()
    
    cameraTween:Play()
    cameraTween.Completed:Wait()
    
    fadeOutTween:Play()
    textFadeOutTween:Play()
    fadeOutTween.Completed:Wait()
    
    camera.CameraSubject = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

playCutscene()

local targetAnimationId = "10471336737" -- The ID of the animation you want to detect
local animationId = "12509505723" -- The ID of the animation you want to play 10469493270

local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

local function playAnimation(character)
    local animation = Instance.new("Animation")
    animation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. animationId

    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if humanoid then
        local animationTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(animation)
        animationTrack:Play() -- Play the animation

local function onAnimationPlayed(animationTrack)
    if animationTrack and animationTrack.Animation and animationTrack.Animation.AnimationId == "rbxassetid://" .. targetAnimationId then
        animationTrack:Stop() -- Stop the target animation
        
        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
        if character then
            playAnimation(character)

local function onCharacterAdded(character)
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if humanoid then
        humanoid.AnimationPlayed:Connect(onAnimationPlayed)

if player.Character then
    onCharacterAdded(player.Character)
player.CharacterAdded:Connect(onCharacterAdded)

local animationIdsToStop = {

    [10469493270] = true,

    [10469630950] = true,

    [10469639222] = true,

    [10469643643] = true,

}


local replacementAnimations = {

    ["10469643643"] = "rbxassetid://17889290569",

    ["10469639222"] = "rbxassetid://17889471098",

    ["10469630950"] = "rbxassetid://17889461810",

    ["10469493270"] = "rbxassetid://17889458563",

}


local queue = {}

local isAnimating = false


local function playReplacementAnimation(animationId)

    if isAnimating then

        table.insert(queue, animationId)

        return


   

    isAnimating = true

    local replacementAnimationId = replacementAnimations[tostring(animationId)]

    if replacementAnimationId then

        local AnimAnim = Instance.new("Animation")

        AnimAnim.AnimationId = replacementAnimationId

        local Anim = humanoid:LoadAnimation(AnimAnim)

        Anim:Play()

       

        Anim.Stopped:Connect(function()

            isAnimating = false

            if #queue > 0 then

                local nextAnimationId = table.remove(queue, 1)

                playReplacementAnimation(nextAnimationId)


        end)

    else

        isAnimating = false




local function stopSpecificAnimations()

    for _, track in ipairs(humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do

        local animationId = tonumber(track.Animation.AnimationId:match("%d+"))

        if animationIdsToStop[animationId] then

            track:Stop()





local function onAnimationPlayed(animationTrack)

    local animationId = tonumber(animationTrack.Animation.AnimationId:match("%d+"))

    if animationIdsToStop[animationId] then

        stopSpecificAnimations()

        animationTrack:Stop()

       

        local replacementAnimationId = replacementAnimations[tostring(animationId)]

        if replacementAnimationId then

            playReplacementAnimation(animationId)





humanoid.AnimationPlayed:Connect(onAnimationPlayed)


local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()

local humanoidRootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")


local function onBodyVelocityAdded(bodyVelocity)

    if bodyVelocity:IsA("BodyVelocity") then

        bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(bodyVelocity.Velocity.X, 0, bodyVelocity.Velocity.Z)




character.DescendantAdded:Connect(onBodyVelocityAdded)


for _, descendant in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do

    onBodyVelocityAdded(descendant)



player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(newCharacter)

    character = newCharacter

    humanoidRootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

    character.DescendantAdded:Connect(onBodyVelocityAdded)

   

    for _, descendant in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do

        onBodyVelocityAdded(descendant)


end)
   end,
})

frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1

local textLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel", screenGui)
textLabel.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0.5, 0.5)
textLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
textLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0.2, 0, 0.1, 0)

textLabel.Text = "äº”æ¡"

textLabel.TextScaled = true
textLabel.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold

    fadeDuration, -- Time
    Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, -- EasingStyle
    Enum.EasingDirection.InOut -- EasingDirection
)

local fadeOutInfo = TweenInfo.new(
    fadeDuration, -- Time
    Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, -- EasingStyle
    Enum.EasingDirection.InOut -- EasingDirection
)

    cutsceneDuration, -- Time
    Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, -- EasingStyle
    Enum.EasingDirection.InOut -- EasingDirection
)

local initialCFrame = humanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -5, 0)

local fadeOutTween = TweenService:Create(frame, fadeOutInfo, {BackgroundTransparency = 1})

local textFadeOutTween = TweenService:Create(textLabel, fadeOutInfo, {TextTransparency = 1})

local function playCutscene()
    camera.CFrame = initialCFrame
    
    fadeInTween:Play()
    textFadeInTween:Play()
    fadeInTween.Completed:Wait()
    
    cameraTween:Play()
    cameraTween.Completed:Wait()
    
    fadeOutTween:Play()
    textFadeOutTween:Play()
    fadeOutTween.Completed:Wait()
    
    camera.CameraSubject = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

local function playAnimation(character)
    stopAllAnimations(character) -- Stop all current animations

    local animation = Instance.new("Animation")

    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

        animationTrack:Play() -- Play the new animation

    if animationTrack and animationTrack.Animation and animationTrack.Animation.AnimationId == "rbxassetid://" .. targetAnimationId then
        animationTrack:Stop() -- Stop the target animation
        
        local character = player.Character
        if character then
            playAnimation(character)

    if humanoid then
        humanoid.AnimationPlayed:Connect(onAnimationPlayed)

local humanoidRootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

local function findDescendant(parent, name)
    local child = parent:FindFirstChild(name)
    if not child then
        for _, descendant in ipairs(parent:GetChildren()) do
            child = findDescendant(descendant, name)
            if child then
                break
    return child

local function duplicateEmitter(originalEmitter)
    local duplicate = originalEmitter:Clone()
    duplicate.Parent = originalEmitter.Parent
    duplicate.Rate = 150  -- Set the rate of the duplicated emitter to 150 initially
    return duplicate

local invisibilityDuration = .55 -- Time the player stays invisible (in seconds)
local invisibleTransparency = 1 -- Transparency when invisible (0 is fully visible, 1 is fully invisible)
local visibleTransparency = 0 -- Transparency when visible

local excludedParts = {
    "HumanoidRootPart",
    "Hitbox_RightArm",
    "Hitbox_RightLeg",
    "Hitbox_LeftLeg",
    "Hitbox_LeftArm",
    "camera",
    "camerarootpart",
    "letterboxtop",
    "letterboxbot",
}

local function isExcluded(part)
    for _, name in ipairs(excludedParts) do
        if part.Name == name then
            return true
    return false

local function turnInvisible()
    for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") and not isExcluded(part) then
            part.Transparency = invisibleTransparency
        elseif (part:IsA("Decal") or part:IsA("Texture")) and not isExcluded(part.Parent) then
            part.Transparency = 1 -- Hide textures/decals fully

local function turnVisible()
    for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") and not isExcluded(part) then
            part.Transparency = visibleTransparency
        elseif (part:IsA("Decal") or part:IsA("Texture")) and not isExcluded(part.Parent) then
            part.Transparency = 0 -- Show textures/decals again

local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local resourcesFolder = replicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Resources", 2) -- Wait for 2 seconds if not immediately found
if resourcesFolder then
    local kjEffectsFolder = resourcesFolder:FindFirstChild("KJEffects")
    if kjEffectsFolder then
        local tpThingEmitter = findDescendant(kjEffectsFolder, "tpthing")
        if tpThingEmitter and tpThingEmitter:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
            local duplicatedEmitter = duplicateEmitter(tpThingEmitter)

            duplicatedEmitter.Parent = humanoidRootPart

            turnInvisible()
            wait(invisibilityDuration)
            turnVisible()

            duplicatedEmitter.Rate = 0
        else
            warn("Could not find tpthing ParticleEmitter or it is not a ParticleEmitter.")
    else
        warn("Could not find KJEffects folder inside Resources.")
else
    warn("Could not find Resources folder inside ReplicatedStorage.")

        animationTrack.Speed = animationSpeed -- Set the animation speed

local function onAnimationPlayed(animationTrack)
    if animationTrack and animationTrack.Animation and animationTrack.Animation.AnimationId == "rbxassetid://" .. targetAnimationId then
        animationTrack:Stop() -- Stop the target animation
        
        local character = player.Character
        if character then
            playAnimation(character)

    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if humanoid then
        humanoid.AnimationPlayed:Connect(onAnimationPlayed)
        

if player.Character then
    onCharacterAdded(player.Character)
